class="css-1lr85n">409 人赞同了该回答</div></div></div><span class="css-z4ujak"></span></div><meta itemprop="image"><meta itemprop="upvoteCount" content="409"><meta itemprop="url" content="https://www.zhihu.com/question/22263777/answer/2689861728"><meta itemprop="dateCreated" content="2022-09-26T02:32:26.000Z"><meta itemprop="dateModified" content="2022-09-26T02:32:26.000Z"><meta itemprop="commentCount" content="18"><div class="RichContent RichContent--unescapable"><span><div class="RichContent-inner"><div class="css-376mun"><span class="RichText ztext CopyrightRichText-richText css-1em8ozd" options="[object Object]" itemprop="text"><p data-first-child="" data-pid="mhflp7-O">不知道大家经历没经历过被 404 支配的恐惧，有过这样惨痛教训的小伙伴一定知道，不能把资源放在一个篮子里，是最基本的操作。</p><p data-pid="-WobDxRH">那不放一个篮子里，就得先把资源保存到本地，影视资源是这样，对于那些质量特别棒、相见恨晚的帖子更是这样，既避免 404，又方便本地管理。</p><p data-pid="uyua4yFR">至于把网页、帖子这些图文保存到本地，最简单的就是「Ctrl+S」，保存成 .html 格式的<span><a class="RichContent-EntityWord css-b7erz1" data-za-not-track-link="true" data-paste-text="true" href="https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E9%A1%B5%E9%9D%A2%E6%96%87%E4%BB%B6&amp;search_source=Entity&amp;hybrid_search_source=Entity&amp;hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2689861728%7D" target="_blank">页面文件<svg width="10px" height="10px" viewBox="0 0 15 15" class="css-1dvsrp"><path d="M10.89 9.477l3.06 3.059a1 1 0 0 1-1.414 1.414l-3.06-3.06a6 6 0 1 1 1.414-1.414zM6 10a4 4 0 1 0 0-8 4 4 0 0 0 0 8z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></a></span>，或者「Ctrl+P」利用浏览器自带的<span><a class="RichContent-EntityWord css-b7erz1" data-za-not-track-link="true" data-paste-text="true" href="https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E8%99%9A%E6%8B%9F%E6%89%93%E5%8D%B0%E6%9C%BA&amp;search_source=Entity&amp;hybrid_search_source=Entity&amp;hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2689861728%7D" target="_blank">虚拟打印机<svg width="10px" height="10px" viewBox="0 0 15 15" class="css-1dvsrp"><path d="M10.89 9.477l3.06 3.059a1 1 0 0 1-1.414 1.414l-3.06-3.06a6 6 0 1 1 1.414-1.414zM6 10a4 4 0 1 0 0-8 4 4 0 0 0 0 8z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></a></span>保存成 PDF 文件。</p><p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p><figure data-size="normal"><noscript><img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-0b20a47365868defcbcf4adb85b48cf2_720w.jpg?source=1def8aca" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1080" data-rawheight="636" data-original-token="v2-0b20a47365868defcbcf4adb85b48cf2" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1080" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0b20a47365868defcbcf4adb85b48cf2_r.jpg?source=1def8aca"/></noscript><div><img src="./test3_files/v2-0b20a47365868defcbcf4adb85b48cf2_1440w.webp" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1080" data-rawheight="636" data-original-token="v2-0b20a47365868defcbcf4adb85b48cf2" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy" width="1080" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0b20a47365868defcbcf4adb85b48cf2_r.jpg?source=1def8aca" data-actualsrc="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-0b20a47365868defcbcf4adb85b48cf2_720w.jpg?source=1def8aca" height="636" data-lazy-status="ok"></div></figure><p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p><p data-pid="VahmhB0N">这样保存简单是简单了，但会碰到许多问题，比如排版丢失、布局错乱，更不要说现在很多网页为了省资源和提高阅读体验，会用上<span><a class="RichContent-EntityWord css-b7erz1" data-za-not-track-link="true" data-paste-text="true" href="https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E6%87%92%E5%8A%A0%E8%BD%BD&amp;search_source=Entity&amp;hybrid_search_source=Entity&amp;hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2689861728%7D" target="_blank">懒加载<svg width="10px" height="10px" viewBox="0 0 15 15" class="css-1dvsrp"><path d="M10.89 9.477l3.06 3.059a1 1 0 0 1-1.414 1.414l-3.06-3.06a6 6 0 1 1 1.414-1.414zM6 10a4 4 0 1 0 0-8 4 4 0 0 0 0 8z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></a></span>的方式，需要我们从头到尾浏览一遍，等素材加载完，才能保存。</p><p data-pid="ArGFmkRU">如果你猴急了，没等加载完就直接保存，难免会翻车。</p><p data-pid="ITBNZkRg">所以这个时候，就要用上我们的 2.0 方案了，即利用脚本或者<span><a class="RichContent-EntityWord css-b7erz1" data-za-not-track-link="true" data-paste-text="true" href="https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E6%B5%8F%E8%A7%88%E5%99%A8%E6%89%A9%E5%B1%95&amp;search_source=Entity&amp;hybrid_search_source=Entity&amp;hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2689861728%7D" target="_blank">浏览器扩展<svg width="10px" height="10px" viewBox="0 0 15 15" class="css-1dvsrp"><path d="M10.89 9.477l3.06 3.059a1 1 0 0 1-1.414 1.414l-3.06-3.06a6 6 0 1 1 1.414-1.414zM6 10a4 4 0 1 0 0-8 4 4 0 0 0 0 8z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></a></span>，来保存网页，我们分享过的工具有「SingleFile」和「Save Page WE」。</p><p data-pid="VE-GuDvP">像苹果官方公众号常用的 SVG 交互动画式排版，都可以原汁原味的保存下来：</p><p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p><figure data-size="normal"><noscript><img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-34b11f336dacbdcf6057bd39453eabb9_720w.gif?source=1def8aca" data-caption="" 还能批量自动保存，以及做笔记或删除<span><a class="RichContent-EntityWord css-b7erz1" data-za-not-track-link="true" data-paste-text="true" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1080" data-rawheight="507" data-original-token="v2-7255fd9fc88d1fa31b03904de36b2218" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy" width="1080" height="507" data-lazy-status="ok"></div></figure><p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p><p data-pid="H_IlS_PL">如果说单纯的图文，其实有这俩扩展就够了，但我最近又有了新的需求，我想把一些利用 CSS\JS 实现的在线工具，一口气也给它保存下来。</p><p data-pid="pPIewn6q">举个栗子，有的时候我们封面图不是有用到 P 站橘白黑的 Logo 风格嘛，其实是我收藏了一个在线生成 P 站 logo 的网页工具：</p><p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p><figure data-size="normal"><noscript><img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-303f7bd0cd333da2a05a788ccdc63105_720w.jpg?source=1def8aca" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1080" data-rawheight="729" data-original-token="v2-303f7bd0cd333da2a05a788ccdc63105" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1080" height="729" data-lazy-status="ok"></div></figure><p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p><p data-pid="MJ5xvpCd">至于为啥突然想把这个在线工具保存到本地？还不是因为我一直用的那个生成器前段时间 404 了。</p><p data-pid="1NbKdY0W">诚然，咱很快又找了个新的，可难免害怕这玩意哪天又凉了，所以才萌生了这样的想法。。。</p><p data-pid="idX3WI9d">不过当我用 SingleFile 和 Save Page WE 保存的时候，发现<span><a class="RichContent-EntityWord css-b7erz1" data-za-not-track-link="true" data-paste-text="true" href="https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E7%BD%91%E9%A1%B5&amp;search_source=Entity&amp;hybrid_search_source=Entity&amp;hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2689861728%7D" target="_blank">网页<svg width="10px" height="10px" viewBox="0 0 15 15" class="css-1dvsrp"><path d="M10.89 9.477l3.06 3.059a1 1 0 0 1-1.414 1.414l-3.06-3.06a6 6 0 1 1 1.414-1.414zM6 10a4 4 0 1 0 0-8 4 4 0 0 0 0 8z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></a></span>虽然能完整的保存下来。</p><p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p><figure data-size="normal"><noscript><img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-e982f929ad65d6278c9589dd55a23277_720w.jpg?source=1def8aca" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1080" data-rawheight="735" data-pid="oZexOlpo">好家伙，利用 ArchiveWeb.page，相当于我把这个别人搭建好的成品小工具，直接就保存到本地了。</p><p data-pid="ol3OW6Qy">看来，我们的本地网页保存方案，是时候进军 3.0 了。</p><p data-pid="2D8QWNhD"><b>具体操作</b></p><p data-pid="TVHAKzaL">ArchiveWeb.page 这个扩展是基于 Chrome 实现的，但我测试过了，只要是 Chromium 内核的浏览器，都可以使用，Edge 也不例外。</p><p data-pid="ap48la2I">有能力访问 Chrome 扩展商店的小伙伴，可以直接去商店下载，当然，我也准备好了最新版的 .<span><a class="RichContent-EntityWord css-b7erz1" data-za-not-track-link="true" data-paste-text="true" href="https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=crx&amp;search_source=Entity&amp;hybrid_search_source=Entity&amp;hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2689861728%7D" target="_blank">crx<svg width="10px" height="10px" viewBox="0 0 15 15" class="css-1dvsrp"><path d="M10.89 9.477l3.06 3.059a1 1 0 0 1-1.414 1.414l-3.06-3.06a6 6 0 1 1 1.414-1.414zM6 10a4 4 0 1 0 0-8 4 4 0 0 0 0 8z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></a></span> 文件。</p><p data-pid="R_pk3pCu">咱们可以通过在扩展管理页面，打开「<span><a class="RichContent-EntityWord css-b7erz1" data-za-not-track-link="true" data-paste-text="true" href="https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E5%BC%80%E5%8F%91%E4%BA%BA%E5%91%98%E6%A8%A1%E5%BC%8F&amp;search_source=Entity&amp;hybrid_search_source=Entity&amp;hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2689861728%7D" target="_blank">开发人员模式<svg width="10px" height="10px" viewBox="0 0 15 15" class="css-1dvsrp"><path d="M10.89 9.477l3.06 3.059a1 1 0 0 1-1.414 1.414l-3.06-3.06a6 6 0 1 1 1.414-1.414zM6 10a4 4 0 1 0 0-8 4 4 0 0 0 0 8z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></a></span>」后，直接拖拽 .crx 到浏览器的方式安装。</p><p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p><figure data-size="normal"><noscript><img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-4cf0df13762fddbe3cfa8afeae4c595b_720w.jpg?source=1def8aca" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1080" data-rawheight="582" data-original-token="v2-4cf0df13762fddbe3cfa8afeae4c595b" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1080" data-original="https://pica.zhimg.com/v2-4cf0df13762fddbe3cfa8afeae4c595b_r.jpg?source=1def8aca"/></noscript><div><img src="data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;582&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1080" data-rawheight="582" data-original-token="v2-4cf0df13762fddbe3cfa8afeae4c595b" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy" width="1080" data-original="https://pica.zhimg.com/v2-4cf0df13762fddbe3cfa8afeae4c595b_r.jpg?source=1def8aca" data-actualsrc="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-4cf0df13762fddbe3cfa8afeae4c595b_720w.jpg?source=1def8aca"></div></figure><p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p><p data-pid="5qzpON2m">安装好扩展，我们就可以开启第一次录制了，点击<span><a class="RichContent-EntityWord css-b7erz1" data-za-not-track-link="true" data-paste-text="true" href="https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E6%89%A9%E5%B1%95%E5%9B%BE%E6%A0%87&amp;search_source=Entity&amp;hybrid_search_source=Entity&amp;hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2689861728%7D" target="_blank">扩展图标<svg width="10px" height="10px" viewBox="0 0 15 15" class="css-1dvsrp"><path d="M10.89 9.477l3.06 3.059a1 1 0 0 1-1.414 1.414l-3.06-3.06a6 6 0 1 1 1.414-1.414zM6 10a4 4 0 1 0 0-8 4 4 0 0 0 0 8z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></a></span>，看到弹窗里有个「Start」的开始按钮。</p><p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p><figure data-size="normal"><noscript><img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-1a12affa0e44288544e538d6e9c026eb_720w.jpg?source=1def8aca" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1080" data-rawheight="523" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-1a12affa0e44288544e538d6e9c026eb_r.jpg?source=1def8aca"/></noscript><div><img src="data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;523&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1080" data-rawheight="523" data-original-token="v2-1a12affa0e44288544e538d6e9c026eb" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy" width="1080" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-1a12affa0e44288544e538d6e9c026eb_r.jpg?source=1def8aca" data-actualsrc="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-1a12affa0e44288544e538d6e9c026eb_720w.jpg?source=1def8aca"></div></figure><p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p><p data-pid="HdJAinrU">开始后，当前网页会重新加载，此时加载的外部资源会一并捕获。</p><p data-pid="LJPyirVY">注意，这里有个调试此<span><a class="RichContent-EntityWord css-b7erz1" data-za-not-track-link="true" data-paste-text="true" href="https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E6%B5%8F%E8%A7%88%E5%99%A8&amp;search_source=Entity&amp;hybrid_search_source=Entity&amp;hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2689861728%7D" target="_blank">浏览器<svg width="10px" height="10px" viewBox="0 0 15 15" class="css-1dvsrp"><path d="M10.89 9.477l3.06 3.059a1 1 0 0 1-1.414 1.414l-3.06-3.06a6 6 0 1 1 1.414-1.414zM6 10a4 4 0 1 0 0-8 4 4 0 0 0 0 8z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></a></span>的通知横幅，如果没有横幅，那证明没有捕获成功，不用做更多的操作。</p><p data-pid="w0FDA0aC">像咱们这个 P 站 logo 生成器，不过是个单一网页，只要等扩展图标变成绿色，点击「Stop」停止录制，我们就保存成功啦。</p><p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p><figure data-size="normal"><noscript><img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-07226d6c986c586a062d97c3837d80b6_720w.jpg?source=1def8aca" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1080" data-rawheight="448" data-original-token="v2-07226d6c986c586a062d97c3837d80b6" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1080" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-07226d6c986c586a062d97c3837d80b6_r.jpg?source=1def8aca"/></noscript><div><img src="data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy" width="1080" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-07226d6c986c586a062d97c3837d80b6_r.jpg?source=1def8aca" data-actualsrc="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-07226d6c986c586a062d97c3837d80b6_720w.jpg?source=1def8aca"></div></figure><p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p><p data-pid="E-7l7hNc">想访问保存好的网页，或是下载到本地，只用重新找到扩展图标，点击里面的主页按钮。</p><p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p><figure data-size="normal"><noscript><img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-15020d42faeb381cd4d5904375c8dae7_720w.jpg?source=1def8aca" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="822" data-rawheight="350" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy" width="822" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-15020d42faeb381cd4d5904375c8dae7_r.jpg?source=1def8aca" data-actualsrc="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-15020d42faeb381cd4d5904375c8dae7_720w.jpg?source=1def8aca"></div></figure><p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p><p data-pid="CrZQtusS">这里存放着我们刚刚保存的网页，可以点击下载图标到以 WACZ 格式保存本地。</p><p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p><figure data-size="normal"><noscript><img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-9d86dab852b8a186fdfc8277e53b7f82_720w.jpg?source=1def8aca" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1080" data-rawheight="353" data-original-token="v2-9d86dab852b8a186fdfc8277e53b7f82" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1080" data-pid="qJRyCLvi">发现没，这里下载的不是一个网页，而是一个合集，如果你保存了多个网页，那点进去就能访问或下载：</p><p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p><figure data-size="normal"><noscript><img data-actualsrc="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-3c36ec0307a563d898bca0a200fbcbc7_720w.jpg?source=1def8aca"></div></figure><p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p><p data-pid="BLwXM4X3">在访问时，会有个目录，这里就是我们保存好的在线工具啦。</p><p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p><figure data-size="normal"><noscript><img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-f3314649a46152c5072a2a21082e211a_720w.gif?source=1def8aca" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1080" data-rawheight="625" data-pid="7hiV3fIO">当然，我们可以在扩展图标准备录制的时候，选择不同的合集：</p><p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p><figure data-size="normal"><noscript><img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-7bc10966f2e8b6f3b748d2a116a6ab11_720w.jpg?source=1def8aca" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="774" data-rawheight="472" data-original-token="v2-7bc10966f2e8b6f3b748d2a116a6ab11" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="774" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-7bc10966f2e8b6f3b748d2a116a6ab11_r.jpg?source=1def8aca"/></noscript><div><img src="data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; data-pid="WeHzndsZ">亦或在主页，导入本地的合集或网页：</p><p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p><figure data-size="normal"><noscript><img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-6623390804f19e2792cc45060b2c9911_720w.jpg?source=1def8aca" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1080" data-rawheight="527" data-original-token="v2-6623390804f19e2792cc45060b2c9911" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1080" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-6623390804f19e2792cc45060b2c9911_r.jpg?source=1def8aca"/></noscript><div><img src="data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy" width="1080" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-6623390804f19e2792cc45060b2c9911_r.jpg?source=1def8aca" data-actualsrc="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-6623390804f19e2792cc45060b2c9911_720w.jpg?source=1def8aca"></div></figure><p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p><p data-pid="YgPxLxqn">不过有一说一，我测试了很多在线工具，ArchiveWeb.page 能保存的，是要前端实现的工具才行。</p><p data-pid="sTPiHmGk">像 OCR、图片抠图这样的在线工具，需要连接服务器才能搞定的网页，ArchiveWeb.page 就帮不上什么忙了。</p><p data-pid="ftdZ3byf">但是，这不妨碍人家强啊，单一网页不说了，轻松搞定，它厉害的点还在于，录制过程中在网页内产生的跳转都能一起捕获。</p><p data-pid="-QanjRmR">举个栗子，公众号的文章合集，我开启录制后，点一下里面的文章：</p><p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p><figure data-size="normal"><noscript><img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-f86d4d7dc2cbd5963a96bd6008c15193_720w.jpg?source=1def8aca" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1080" data-rawheight="762" data-original-token="v2-f86d4d7dc2cbd5963a96bd6008c15193" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1080" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-f86d4d7dc2cbd5963a96bd6008c15193_r.jpg?source=1def8aca"/></noscript><div><img src="data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy" width="1080" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-f86d4d7dc2cbd5963a96bd6008c15193_r.jpg?source=1def8aca" data-actualsrc="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-f86d4d7dc2cbd5963a96bd6008c15193_720w.jpg?source=1def8aca"></div></figure><p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p><p data-pid="7_sVhzfK">录制后，你会发现，连点进去的文章都捕获了，还能从上一个网页直接跳转：</p><p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p><figure data-size="normal"><noscript><img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-a4995d0e802999e99abac32a11a67ace_720w.gif?source=1def8aca" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1080" data-rawheight="625" data-original-token="v2-a4995d0e802999e99abac32a11a67ace" data-thumbnail="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-a4995d0e802999e99abac32a11a67ace_720w.jpg?source=1def8aca" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1080" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-a4995d0e802999e99abac32a11a67ace_r.jpg?source=1def8aca"/></noscript><div><div class="GifPlayer css-1isopsn" data-size="normal" css-d39tw7"><svg width="50" height="50" viewBox="0 0 60 60" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g stroke="none" stroke-width="1" fill="none" fill-rule="evenodd"><ellipse fill="#000" opacity="0.45" cx="30" cy="30" rx="30" ry="30"></ellipse><ellipse stroke="#FFF" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" opacity="0.5" cx="30" cy="30" rx="26" ry="26"></ellipse></g><svg x="16" y="18.5"><g fill="#fff"><path x="100" y="100" d="M12.8422852,12.9814453 L12.8422852,11.3994141 L7.63916016,11.3994141 L7.63916016,13.0517578 L10.9086914,13.0517578 L10.9086914,13.3242188 C10.8911133,15.2050781 9.46728516,16.4707031 7.39306641,16.4707031 C5.01123047,16.4707031 3.51708984,14.625 3.51708984,11.6367188 C3.51708984,8.70117188 5.00244141,6.84667969 7.34912109,6.84667969 data-pid="GCoqPji_">如果你要录制的是社交媒体平台，有那中<span><a class="RichContent-EntityWord css-b7erz1" data-za-not-track-link="true" data-paste-text="true" href="https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E7%80%91%E5%B8%83%E6%B5%81&amp;search_source=Entity&amp;hybrid_search_source=Entity&amp;hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2689861728%7D" target="_blank">瀑布流<svg width="10px" height="10px" viewBox="0 0 15 15" class="css-1dvsrp"><path d="M10.89 9.477l3.06 3.059a1 1 0 0 1-1.414 1.414l-3.06-3.06a6 6 0 1 1 1.414-1.414zM6 10a4 4 0 1 0 0-8 4 4 0 0 0 0 8z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></a></span>自动加载，记得勾选「Start With Autopilot」，只有这样才能捕获更复杂的网站交互。</p><p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p><figure data-size="normal"><noscript><img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-e90fd9df2812567f9aa401deabc227d2_720w.jpg?source=1def8aca" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="784" data-rawheight="299" data-original-token="v2-e90fd9df2812567f9aa401deabc227d2" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="784" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-e90fd9df2812567f9aa401deabc227d2_r.jpg?source=1def8aca"/></noscript><div><img src="data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy" width="784" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-e90fd9df2812567f9aa401deabc227d2_r.jpg?source=1def8aca" data-actualsrc="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-e90fd9df2812567f9aa401deabc227d2_720w.jpg?source=1def8aca"></div></figure><p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p><p data-pid="WsHHsUgB">要说 ArchiveWeb.page 有什么不足，大概就是这玩意没有汉化了，但相信聪明如你，看了这篇文章，摸索个两分钟就搞定了。</p><p data-pid="jcWUCfN-"><b>结语</b></p><p data-pid="rabLZ-g0">虽说是本地保存 3.0，但实话实说，ArchiveWeb.page 导出的 WACZ 格式没有直接 HTML 那样好管理，多半还要借助<span><a class="RichContent-EntityWord css-b7erz1" data-za-not-track-link="true" data-paste-text="true" href="https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E6%89%A9%E5%B1%95%E8%AE%BF%E9%97%AE&amp;search_source=Entity&amp;hybrid_search_source=Entity&amp;hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2689861728%7D" target="_blank">扩展访问<svg width="10px" height="10px" viewBox="0 0 15 15" class="css-1dvsrp"><path d="M10.89 9.477l3.06 3.059a1 1 0 0 1-1.414 1.414l-3.06-3.06a6 6 0 1 1 1.414-1.414zM6 10a4 4 0 1 0 0-8 4 4 0 0 0 0 8z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></a></span>。</p><p data-pid="ZKaak5A2">所以我的建议还是和 SingleFile 等扩展搭配着来用，如果像保存的网页不用交互，那怎么保存都行；如果需要交互，ArchiveWeb.page 是不二之选。</p><p data-pid="F5Te7VnR">这么有趣还有用的工具，你还不快去试试？老规矩，我把 ArchiveWeb.page 放后台了，感兴趣的小伙伴自取吧。</p><p data-pid="eWV-_7T9"><a href="https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//wwz.lanzouw.com/iqi9n0cd82yf" class=" external" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer"><span class="invisible">https://</span><span class="visible">wwz.lanzouw.com/iqi9n0c</span><span class="invisible">d82yf</span><span class="ellipsis"></span></a></p><p data-pid="elDRkcBr">本文首发于微信公众号网罗灯下黑（wldxh8），未经授权请勿转载！</p><p data-pid="X-faX-yx">一如既往感谢各位小伙伴的支持和关注！</p></span></div></div></span><div><div class="ContentItem-time"><a content="https://www.zhihu.com/question/22263777/answer/111807670"><meta itemprop="dateCreated" content="2016-07-18T08:17:30.000Z"><meta itemprop="dateModified" content="2016-07-18T08:17:30.000Z"><meta itemprop="commentCount" content="40"><div class="RichContent RichContent--unescapable"><span><div class="RichContent-inner"><div class="css-376mun"><span class="RichText ztext CopyrightRichText-richText css-1em8ozd" options="[object Object]" itemprop="text"><p data-first-child="" data-pid="uUf7yTFq">        在 Chrome <span><a class="RichContent-EntityWord css-b7erz1" data-za-not-track-link="true" data-paste-text="true" href="https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E5%9C%B0%E5%9D%80%E6%A0%8F&amp;search_source=Entity&amp;hybrid_search_source=Entity&amp;hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A111807670%7D" target="_blank">地址栏<svg width="10px" height="10px" viewBox="0 0 15 15" class="css-1dvsrp"><path d="M10.89 9.477l3.06 3.059a1 1 0 0 1-1.414 1.414l-3.06-3.06a6 6 0 1 1 1.414-1.414zM6 10a4 4 0 1 0 0-8 4 4 0 0 0 0 8z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></a></span>中键入“<strong>chrome://flags</strong>”，回车，这是一个 Chrome 的功能配置页面，项目比较多，我们通过 Ctrl+F 来搜索“mhtml”，找到“将网页另存为 MHTML”这一项，然后点击下方的“启用”即可。</p><p data-pid="X77awP2B">　　此时打开任一网页，右击“另存为”，将默认保存为.mhtml文件，即<span><a class="RichContent-EntityWord css-b7erz1" data-za-not-track-link="true" data-paste-text="true" 4 4 0 0 0 0 8z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></a></span>。</p><p data-pid="jTP-yd8v">来源：<a href="https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.ihacksoft.com/chrome-save-mht.html" class=" wrap class="css-z4ujak"></span></div><meta itemprop="image"><meta itemprop="upvoteCount" content="67"><meta itemprop="url" content="https://www.zhihu.com/question/22263777/answer/129753751"><meta itemprop="dateCreated" content="2016-11-04T01:42:59.000Z"><meta itemprop="dateModified" content="2016-11-04T01:42:59.000Z"><meta itemprop="commentCount" content="6"><div class="RichContent RichContent--unescapable"><span><div class="RichContent-inner"><div class="css-376mun"><span class="RichText ztext CopyrightRichText-richText css-1em8ozd" options="[object Object]" itemprop="text"><p data-first-child="" data-pid="WW70U-7-">文章保存备份工作是非常重要的，万一哪天平台就给你删除了呢？（以往的<span><a class="RichContent-EntityWord css-b7erz1" data-za-not-track-link="true" data-paste-text="true" href="https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E5%8D%9A%E5%AE%A2&amp;search_source=Entity&amp;hybrid_search_source=Entity&amp;hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A129753751%7D" target="_blank">博客<svg width="10px" height="10px" viewBox="0 0 15 15" class="css-1dvsrp"><path d="M10.89 9.477l3.06 3.059a1 1 0 0 1-1.414 1.414l-3.06-3.06a6 6 0 1 1 1.414-1.414zM6 10a4 4 0 1 0 0-8 4 4 0 0 0 0 8z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></a></span>，曾经的云盘，现在的微博，此刻的知乎······哪一个不是一样）现在的互联网，谁都不能信，只能信自己。</p><p data-pid="H2XOJ6u-">以我自己的专栏文章为例。</p><p data-pid="KdQJ1XhQ">不要用什么Pocket和<span><a class="RichContent-EntityWord css-b7erz1" data-za-not-track-link="true" data-paste-text="true" href="https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E5%8D%B0%E8%B1%A1%E7%AC%94%E8%AE%B0&amp;search_source=Entity&amp;hybrid_search_source=Entity&amp;hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A129753751%7D" target="_blank">印象笔记<svg width="10px" height="10px" viewBox="0 0 15 15" class="css-1dvsrp"><path d="M10.89 9.477l3.06 3.059a1 1 0 0 1-1.414 1.414l-3.06-3.06a6 6 0 1 1 1.414-1.414zM6 10a4 4 0 1 0 0-8 4 4 0 0 0 0 8z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></a></span>来备份，这种方式备份无法解决问题。</p><p data-pid="lJOjzB4c">今天讲一种PDF和<span><a class="RichContent-EntityWord css-b7erz1" data-za-not-track-link="true" data-paste-text="true" href="https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E7%BD%91%E9%A1%B5%E5%A4%87%E4%BB%BD&amp;search_source=Entity&amp;hybrid_search_source=Entity&amp;hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A129753751%7D" target="_blank">网页备份<svg width="10px" height="10px" viewBox="0 0 15 15" class="css-1dvsrp"><path d="M10.89 9.477l3.06 3.059a1 1 0 0 1-1.414 1.414l-3.06-3.06a6 6 0 1 1 1.414-1.414zM6 10a4 4 0 1 0 0-8 4 4 0 0 0 0 8z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></a></span>两者结合保存备份的方式，这种方式较以上方式或其它方式更加完美，因为PDF的图片无法完美导出，而网页保存的方式可以直接将所有图片导出，两者结合起来备份几乎完美。目前来看，我认为网页打印PDF保存+网页直接保存是目前最便捷也是最好的方式之一，肯定有更完美的方式，但对大多数人来说，这更便捷。</p><p data-pid="mO1mTKA_">Ctrl+P就搞定了，如图所示（已经有人讲过了，但貌似讲得太长，本就是几张图的问题）</p><p data-pid="Cgee7JMA"><i>Ctrl+P网页打印PDF保存方式</i></p><figure><noscript><img 3.0，但实话实说，ArchiveWeb.page 导出的 WACZ 格式没有直接 HTML 那样好管理，多半还要借助扩展访问。\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp data-pid=\"ZKaak5A2\"\u003E所以我的建议还是和 SingleFile 等扩展搭配着来用，如果像保存的网页不用交互，那怎么保存都行；如果需要交互，ArchiveWeb.page
